I would like to ask the room manager, every time I go out, the eldest sister always asks me if I want to clean the room, whether you have checked out, etc. Is it the hotel's sop process? And the voice of talking/working in the aisle of the guest area is also loud.
2. For inquiring about relevant epidemic prevention documents in Chongqing, the price of nucleic acid shall not exceed 16 yuan. But the nucleic acid on the first floor of your hotel is 24 yuan per person! Why? ! I didn't do it, I went outside to do it for 3.5/person, so I didn't pay for the screenshots.
3. There are children swimming in the pool, and there are parents watching next to them, but the parents are also looking at their mobile phones. There is no lifeguard in the entire pool. Does this meet swimming pool business standards? ! The spin dryer and hand dryer in the dressing room are obviously not designed for use. Using the spin dryer will inevitably induce the hand dryer to work. Isn't this a waste of energy? There are also suggestions for strengthening energy control, such as massage pools.
4. The hotel body wash is basically used two to three times. It is recommended to add an extra bottle, after all, it is summer. Of course you need to call and it will be delivered quickly.
5. As a ten-year hotel, hardware aging cannot be ignored, such as the clarity of TV signals. And why should the door of the minibar be locked? There should be a small refrigerator inside. The weather in Chongqing is so hot, can you open the small refrigerator so that guests can prepare some cold drinks?
In short, the hotel experience is not strong, it is not worth recommending and choosing next time.
